# Excalidraw Data

## Text Elements
the angle of the arch that has length equal to the radius ^FIqhvfTy

negative of reciprocal ^6vxVIlSm

smaller and smaller rectangles ^f3Ew2ldU

a matrix that has the same amount of columns and rows ^cup4pAgl

matrices are vectors with only one column and n rows where n is the
"dimensions" of the vector ^IL054I5Z
